      ecmaVersion: 2020,

FILE: ./src/App.tsx
========================================

import { lazy, Suspense } from "react";
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { BrowserRouter, Route, Routes } from "react-router-dom";
import { Toaster as Sonner } from "@/components/ui/sonner";
import { Toaster } from "@/components/ui/toaster";
import { TooltipProvider } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";
import { AuthProvider } from "@/contexts/AuthContext";

const Index = lazy(() => import("./pages/Index.tsx"));
const NotFound = lazy(() => import("./pages/NotFound.tsx"));

const queryClient = new QueryClient();

const App = () => (
  <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
    <AuthProvider>
      <TooltipProvider>
        <Toaster />
        <Sonner />
        <BrowserRouter>
          <main>
            <Suspense fallback={<div className="min-h-screen bg-background flex items-center justify-center"><div className="animate-pulse text-muted-foreground">Loading...</div></div>}>
              <Routes>
                <Route path="/" element={<Index />} />
                <Route path="*" element={<NotFound />} />
              </Routes>
            </Suspense>
          </main>
        </BrowserRouter>
      </TooltipProvider>
    </AuthProvider>
  </QueryClientProvider>
);

export default App;

FILE: ./src/components/AppDashboard.tsx
========================================

import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Sun, Calendar, BarChart3, Brain, LogOut, CreditCard, Lock, Crown } from "lucide-react";
import { getTrialDaysRemaining } from "@/lib/store";
import { isFeatureLocked } from "@/lib/plans";

interface AppDashboardProps {
  trialStart: string | null;
  onNavigate: (view: string) => void;
  dayOfWeek: number;
  isPaid: boolean;
  onSignOut?: () => void;
}

export function AppDashboard({ trialStart, onNavigate, dayOfWeek, isPaid, onSignOut }: AppDashboardProps) {
  const daysLeft = getTrialDaysRemaining(trialStart);
  const dayName = ['Sunday', 'Monday', 'Tuesday', 'Wednesday', 'Thursday', 'Friday', 'Saturday'][dayOfWeek];

  const isSunday = dayOfWeek === 0;
  const isSaturday = dayOfWeek === 6;

  const matrixLocked = isFeatureLocked('hasEisenhowerMatrix', isPaid);
  const weeklyCloseLocked = isFeatureLocked('hasWeeklyClose', isPaid);
  const statsLocked = isFeatureLocked('hasWeeklyStats', isPaid);

  const quickLinks = [
    { label: "Brain Dump", icon: Brain, view: "braindump", desc: "Add or review items", locked: false },
    { label: "Daily View", icon: Sun, view: "daily", desc: "Morning focus", locked: false },
    { label: "Weekly Close", icon: Calendar, view: "saturday", desc: "Saturday review", locked: weeklyCloseLocked },
    { label: "Week Stats", icon: BarChart3, view: "saturday", desc: "See your numbers", locked: statsLocked },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background px-6 py-12">
      <div className="max-w-2xl mx-auto">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-10">
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold">WeeklyFlow — Your Weekly Dashboard</h1>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
              {dayName}
              {isPaid ? (
                <span className="ml-2 inline-flex items-center gap-1 text-primary font-medium">
                  <Crown className="h-3 w-3" /> Pro
                </span>
              ) : (
                ` · ${daysLeft} day${daysLeft !== 1 ? "s" : ""} left in trial`
              )}
            </p>
          </div>
          <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" aria-label="Sign out" onClick={onSignOut || (() => onNavigate('landing'))}>
            <LogOut className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>

        {/* Trial / Upgrade banner */}
        {!isPaid && (
          <div className="surface-warm rounded-xl p-4 mb-8 flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <p className="text-sm font-medium">
                {daysLeft <= 3
                  ? <><strong>{daysLeft} day{daysLeft !== 1 ? "s" : ""} left</strong> in your free trial</>
                  : <>{daysLeft} day{daysLeft !== 1 ? "s" : ""} remaining in your free trial</>
                }
              </p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">Some features are limited on the free plan</p>
            </div>
            <Button size="sm" variant="default" onClick={() => onNavigate('paywall')}>
              <CreditCard className="h-4 w-4 mr-1" /> Upgrade
            </Button>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Today's action */}
        <div className="surface-raised rounded-2xl p-8 mb-6 border animate-fade-up">
          <h2 className="font-display text-xl font-semibold mb-2">
            {isSunday ? "Sunday Setup" : isSaturday ? "Saturday Close" : "Today's Focus"}
          </h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-6">
            {isSunday ? "Plan your week with a brain dump and set your intentions." :
             isSaturday && weeklyCloseLocked ? "Upgrade to Pro to unlock Saturday reviews." :
             isSaturday ? "Review your week, see your stats, and close out." :
             "Pick your Daily 3 and set your Commander's Intent."}
          </p>
          {isSaturday && weeklyCloseLocked ? (
            <Button variant="default" size="lg" onClick={() => onNavigate('paywall')}>
              <Lock className="mr-2 h-5 w-5" /> Unlock with Pro
            </Button>
          ) : (
            <Button
              variant="hero"
              size="lg"
              onClick={() => onNavigate(isSunday ? 'braindump' : isSaturday ? 'saturday' : 'daily')}
            >
              {isSunday ? <><Brain className="mr-2 h-5 w-5" /> Start Brain Dump</> :
               isSaturday ? <><BarChart3 className="mr-2 h-5 w-5" /> Review Week</> :
               <><Sun className="mr-2 h-5 w-5" /> Open Morning</> }
            </Button>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Quick links */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
          {quickLinks.map((link, i) => (
            <button
              key={link.label}
              onClick={() => link.locked ? onNavigate('paywall') : onNavigate(link.view)}
              className={`surface-raised rounded-xl p-5 text-left border hover:shadow-md transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.97] animate-fade-up ${link.locked ? 'opacity-60' : ''}`}
              style={{ animationDelay: `${0.15 + i * 0.06}s` }}
            >
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                <link.icon className={`h-5 w-5 ${link.locked ? 'text-muted-foreground' : 'text-primary'}`} />
                {link.locked && <Lock className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />}
              </div>
              <p className="font-display font-semibold text-sm">{link.label}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{link.locked ? "Pro only" : link.desc}</p>
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


========================================
FILE: ./src/components/AuthScreen.tsx
========================================

import { useState } from "react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { useAuth } from "@/contexts/AuthContext";
import { ArrowLeft, Mail, Lock, Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
import { toast } from "sonner";

interface AuthScreenProps {
  onBack: () => void;
}

export function AuthScreen({ onBack }: AuthScreenProps) {
  const { signUp, signIn } = useAuth();
  const [isSignUp, setIsSignUp] = useState(true);
  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
  const [password, setPassword] = useState("");
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!email || !password) return;
    setLoading(true);

    try {
      const { error } = isSignUp
        ? await signUp(email, password)
        : await signIn(email, password);

      if (error) {
        toast.error(error.message);
      } else {
        toast.success(isSignUp ? "Account created successfully" : "Signed in successfully");
      }
    } catch {
      toast.error("Something went wrong. Please try again.");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background flex items-center justify-center px-6 py-12">
      <div className="max-w-sm w-full animate-fade-up">
        <button
          onClick={onBack}
          className="flex items-center gap-1 text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors mb-8"
        >
          <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" /> Back
        </button>

        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-2">
          {isSignUp ? "Create your WeeklyFlow account" : "Welcome back to WeeklyFlow"}
        </h1>
        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-8">
          {isSignUp
            ? "Start your 7-day free trial. No credit card required."
            : "Sign in to continue planning your weeks."}
        </p>

        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
          <div className="relative">
            <label htmlFor="auth-email" className="sr-only">Email address</label>
            <Mail className="absolute left-3 top-3 h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" aria-hidden="true" />
            <Input
              id="auth-email"
              type="email"
              placeholder="Email address"
              value={email}
              onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
              className="pl-10"
              required
            />
          </div>
          <div className="relative">
            <label htmlFor="auth-password" className="sr-only">Password</label>
            <Lock className="absolute left-3 top-3 h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" aria-hidden="true" />
            <Input
              id="auth-password"
              type="password"
              placeholder="Password"
              value={password}
              onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
              className="pl-10"
              minLength={6}
              required
            />
          </div>
          <Button type="submit" variant="hero" size="lg" className="w-full" disabled={loading} aria-label={isSignUp ? "Create account" : "Sign in"}>
            {loading ? <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" aria-hidden="true" /> : isSignUp ? "Create Account" : "Sign In"}
          </Button>
        </form>

        <p className="text-sm text-center text-muted-foreground mt-6">
          {isSignUp ? "Already have an account?" : "Need an account?"}{" "}
          <button
            onClick={() => setIsSignUp(!isSignUp)}
            className="text-primary font-medium hover:underline"
          >
            {isSignUp ? "Sign in" : "Sign up"}
          </button>
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


========================================
FILE: ./src/components/BrainDump.tsx
========================================

import { useState } from "react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { ArrowRight, Plus, X, ArrowLeft, Briefcase, Heart, EyeOff, AlertTriangle } from "lucide-react";
import { BrainDumpItem, generateId, type TaskSource } from "@/lib/store";
import { getBrainDumpLimit } from "@/lib/plans";

interface BrainDumpProps {
  items: BrainDumpItem[];
  weekId: string;
  onUpdate: (items: BrainDumpItem[]) => void;
  onContinue: () => void;
  onBack?: () => void;
  isReactive?: boolean;
  isPro?: boolean;
}

const layers = [
  { key: 'work' as const, label: 'Work Responsibilities', icon: Briefcase, prompt: 'What work tasks, projects, deadlines or commitments are on your mind?' },
  { key: 'personal' as const, label: 'Personal Commitments', icon: Heart, prompt: 'What personal tasks, errands, social commitments or family obligations are weighing on you?' },
  { key: 'avoiding' as const, label: 'Things Being Avoided', icon: EyeOff, prompt: 'What have you been putting off? What keeps getting moved to "tomorrow"?' },
  { key: 'worry' as const, label: 'Things Causing Worry', icon: AlertTriangle, prompt: 'What anxieties or worries are occupying mental space — even if you can\'t act on them right now?' },
];

export function BrainDump({ items, weekId, onUpdate, onContinue, onBack, isReactive, isPro = false }: BrainDumpProps) {
  const [activeLayer, setActiveLayer] = useState(0);
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");

  const layer = layers[activeLayer];
  const layerItems = items.filter(i => i.layer === layer.key);
  const source: TaskSource = isReactive ? 'reactive' : 'intentional';
  const limit = getBrainDumpLimit(isPro);
  const weekItems = items.filter(i => i.weekId === weekId);
  const atLimit = weekItems.length >= limit;

  const addItem = () => {
    if (!input.trim()) return;
    if (atLimit) return;
    const newItem: BrainDumpItem = {
      id: generateId(),
      text: input.trim(),
      layer: layer.key,
      source,
      status: 'pending',
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      weekId,
    };
    onUpdate([...items, newItem]);
    setInput("");
  };

  const removeItem = (id: string) => {
    onUpdate(items.filter(i => i.id !== id));
  };

  const totalItems = weekItems.length;

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background px-6 py-12">
      <div className="max-w-2xl mx-auto">
        <div className="mb-10 animate-fade-up">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-2">
            {onBack && (
              <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={onBack} aria-label="Go back">
                <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" aria-hidden="true" />
              </Button>
            )}
            <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold">Master Brain Dump — empty your mind</h1>
          </div>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground text-center">
            {isReactive ? "Add new items that have come in" : "Empty your mind. Go through each layer."}
          </p>
          {!isPro && (
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground text-center mt-1">
              {totalItems}/{limit} items used · <span className="text-primary">Upgrade for unlimited</span>
            </p>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Layer tabs */}
        <div className="flex gap-2 mb-8 overflow-x-auto pb-2">
          {layers.map((l, i) => (
            <button
              key={l.key}
              onClick={() => setActiveLayer(i)}
              className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium whitespace-nowrap transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.97] ${
                i === activeLayer
                  ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-sm"
                  : "surface-warm text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
              }`}
            >
              <l.icon className="h-4 w-4" />
              {l.label}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Prompt */}
        <div className="surface-warm rounded-xl p-5 mb-6 animate-fade-up">
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground italic">{layer.prompt}</p>
        </div>

        {/* Input */}
        <div className="flex gap-3 mb-6">
          <label htmlFor="braindump-input" className="sr-only">Add a brain dump item</label>
          <input
            id="braindump-input"
            type="text"
            value={input}
            onChange={e => setInput(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && addItem()}
            placeholder={atLimit ? "Item limit reached — upgrade to Pro" : "Type something on your mind..."}
            disabled={atLimit}
            className="flex-1 h-12 px-4 rounded-lg border bg-background text-foreground font-body placeholder:text-muted-foreground disabled:opacity-50"
          />
          <Button onClick={addItem} size="lg" disabled={atLimit} aria-label="Add item">
            <Plus className="h-4 w-4" aria-hidden="true" />
          </Button>
        </div>

        {/* Items */}
        <div className="space-y-2 mb-10">
          {layerItems.map((item, i) => (
            <div
              key={item.id}
              className="surface-raised rounded-lg px-4 py-3 flex items-center justify-between gap-3 animate-fade-up"
              style={{ animationDelay: `${i * 0.05}s` }}
            >
              <span className="text-sm">{item.text}</span>
              <button onClick={() => removeItem(item.id)} aria-label={`Remove "${item.text}"`} className="text-muted-foreground hover:text-destructive transition-colors">
                <X className="h-4 w-4" aria-hidden="true" />
              </button>
            </div>
          ))}
          {layerItems.length === 0 && (
            <p className="text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground py-8">No items yet. Start typing above.</p>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Continue */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{totalItems} items total</p>
          <Button variant="hero" size="lg" onClick={onContinue} disabled={totalItems === 0}>
            Sort into Matrix <ArrowRight className="ml-2 h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


========================================
FILE: ./src/components/DailyView.tsx
========================================

import { useState } from "react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Sun, Moon, Star, Check, ArrowRight, ArrowLeft, Plus, X, ChevronDown } from "lucide-react";
import { BrainDumpItem, DailyEntry, generateId, type TaskStatus } from "@/lib/store";

interface DailyViewProps {
  items: BrainDumpItem[];
  dailyEntry: DailyEntry | null;
  onSaveEntry: (entry: DailyEntry) => void;
  onUpdateItems: (items: BrainDumpItem[]) => void;
  onAddReactive: () => void;
  onBack?: () => void;
}

export function DailyView({ items, dailyEntry, onSaveEntry, onUpdateItems, onAddReactive, onBack }: DailyViewProps) {
  const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
  const dayName = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'long' });
  const [mode, setMode] = useState<'morning' | 'evening'>(dailyEntry?.daily3.length ? 'evening' : 'morning');
  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<string[]>(dailyEntry?.daily3 || []);
  const [intent, setIntent] = useState(dailyEntry?.commandersIntent || "");
  const [win, setWin] = useState(dailyEntry?.win || "");
  const [statuses, setStatuses] = useState<Record<string, TaskStatus>>({});

  const doItems = items.filter(i => i.category === 'do' && i.status === 'pending');

  const toggleSelect = (id: string) => {
    if (selected.includes(id)) {
      setSelected(selected.filter(s => s !== id));
    } else if (selected.length < 3) {
      setSelected([...selected, id]);
    }
  };

  const saveMorning = () => {
    const entry: DailyEntry = {
      date: today,
      daily3: selected,
      commandersIntent: intent,
      win: "",
      completed: false,
    };
    onSaveEntry(entry);
    setMode('evening');
  };

  const saveEvening = () => {
    // Update item statuses
    const updatedItems = items.map(item => {
      const st = statuses[item.id];
      if (st === 'done') return { ...item, status: 'done' as TaskStatus };
      if (st) return { ...item, status: st };
      return item;
    });
    onUpdateItems(updatedItems);

    const entry: DailyEntry = {
      date: today,
      daily3: selected,
      commandersIntent: intent,
      win,
      completed: true,
    };
    onSaveEntry(entry);
  };

  if (mode === 'morning') {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background px-6 py-12">
        <div className="max-w-2xl mx-auto">
          <div className="text-center mb-10 animate-fade-up">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-3 mb-2">
              {onBack && (
                <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={onBack}>
                  <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
                </Button>
              )}
              <div className="w-14 h-14 rounded-2xl bg-accent/20 flex items-center justify-center">
                <Sun className="h-6 w-6 text-accent-foreground" />
              </div>
            </div>
            <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-1">Good Morning — plan your day</h1>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground">{dayName} - Pick your Daily 3</p>
          </div>

          <div className="mb-6">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
              <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider">Your "Do" List</h3>
              <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={onAddReactive}>
                <Plus className="h-4 w-4 mr-1" /> Add New
              </Button>
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-2">
              {doItems.map(item => (
                <button
                  key={item.id}
                  onClick={() => toggleSelect(item.id)}
                  className={`w-full text-left px-4 py-3 rounded-lg flex items-center gap-3 transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.98] ${
                    selected.includes(item.id)
                      ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-sm"
                      : "surface-raised border hover:shadow-sm"
                  }`}
                >
                  <div className={`w-5 h-5 rounded-full border-2 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${
                    selected.includes(item.id) ? "border-primary-foreground bg-primary-foreground/20" : "border-border"
                  }`}>
                    {selected.includes(item.id) && <Check className="h-3 w-3" />}
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-sm">{item.text}</span>
                  {item.source === 'reactive' && (
                    <span className="ml-auto text-xs opacity-60 bg-warning/20 px-2 py-0.5 rounded">Reactive</span>
                  )}
                </button>
              ))}
              {doItems.length === 0 && (
                <p className="text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground py-8">All caught up! Add new items if needed.</p>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>

          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-6">{selected.length}/3 selected</p>

          <div className="mb-10">
            <label htmlFor="commanders-intent" className="text-sm font-medium mb-2 block">Commander's Intent — your one non-negotiable today</label>
            <input
              id="commanders-intent"
              type="text"
              value={intent}
              onChange={e => setIntent(e.target.value)}
              placeholder="If I do only one thing today, it must be..."
              className="w-full h-12 px-4 rounded-lg border bg-background text-foreground font-body placeholder:text-muted-foreground"
            />
          </div>

          <div className="flex justify-end">
            <Button variant="hero" size="lg" onClick={saveMorning} disabled={selected.length === 0 || !intent.trim()}>
              Lock In My Day <ArrowRight className="ml-2 h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  // Evening mode
  const selectedItems = items.filter(i => selected.includes(i.id));

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background px-6 py-12">
      <div className="max-w-2xl mx-auto">
        <div className="text-center mb-10 animate-fade-up">
          <div className="w-14 h-14 rounded-2xl bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
            <Moon className="h-6 w-6 text-primary" />
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-1">Evening Close — review today</h1>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground">{dayName} · How did it go?</p>
        </div>

        <div className="space-y-3 mb-8">
          {selectedItems.map(item => (
            <div key={item.id} className="surface-raised rounded-lg p-4">
              <p className="text-sm mb-3">{item.text}</p>
              <div className="flex gap-2">
                {(['done', 'partial', 'not-done'] as TaskStatus[]).map(st => (
                  <button
                    key={st}
                    onClick={() => setStatuses({ ...statuses, [item.id]: st })}
                    className={`px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-xs font-medium transition-all active:scale-[0.97] ${
                      statuses[item.id] === st
                        ? st === 'done' ? 'bg-success text-success-foreground' :
                          st === 'partial' ? 'bg-warning text-warning-foreground' :
                          'bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground'
                        : 'bg-muted text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted/80'
                    }`}
                  >
                    {st === 'done' ? 'Done' : st === 'partial' ? 'Partial' : 'Not Done'}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        <div className="mb-10">
          <label htmlFor="todays-win" className="text-sm font-medium mb-2 flex items-center gap-2">
            <Star className="h-4 w-4 text-accent" aria-hidden="true" />
            Today's Win — no matter how small
          </label>
          <input
            id="todays-win"
            type="text"
            value={win}
            onChange={e => setWin(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="What's one thing that went well today?"
            className="w-full h-12 px-4 rounded-lg border bg-background text-foreground font-body placeholder:text-muted-foreground"
          />
        </div>

        <div className="flex justify-end">
          <Button variant="hero" size="lg" onClick={saveEvening} disabled={!win.trim()}>
            Close the Day <Check className="ml-2 h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


========================================
FILE: ./src/components/EisenhowerMatrix.tsx
========================================

import { useState } from "react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { ArrowRight, ArrowLeft, Zap, Clock, Users, Trash2 } from "lucide-react";
import { BrainDumpItem, EisenhowerCategory } from "@/lib/store";

interface EisenhowerMatrixProps {
  items: BrainDumpItem[];
  onUpdate: (items: BrainDumpItem[]) => void;
  onContinue: () => void;
  onBack?: () => void;
}

const categories: { key: EisenhowerCategory; label: string; desc: string; icon: typeof Zap; color: string }[] = [
  { key: 'do', label: 'Do', desc: 'Urgent & Important', icon: Zap, color: 'bg-primary/10 text-primary border-primary/20' },
  { key: 'schedule', label: 'Schedule', desc: 'Important, Not Urgent', icon: Clock, color: 'bg-accent/20 text-accent-foreground border-accent/30' },
  { key: 'delegate', label: 'Delegate', desc: 'Urgent, Not Important', icon: Users, color: 'bg-warning/20 text-warning-foreground border-warning/30' },
  { key: 'drop', label: 'Drop', desc: 'Neither', icon: Trash2, color: 'bg-muted text-muted-foreground border-border' },
];

export function EisenhowerMatrix({ items, onUpdate, onContinue, onBack }: EisenhowerMatrixProps) {
  const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const unsorted = items.filter(i => !i.category);

  const assignCategory = (itemId: string, category: EisenhowerCategory) => {
    onUpdate(items.map(i => i.id === itemId ? { ...i, category } : i));
    setSelectedItem(null);
  };

  const allSorted = unsorted.length === 0;

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background px-6 py-12">
      <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
        <div className="text-center mb-10 animate-fade-up">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-3 mb-2">
            {onBack && (
              <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={onBack}>
                <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
              </Button>
            )}
            <h2 className="text-3xl font-bold">Eisenhower Matrix</h2>
          </div>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground">Sort each item. {unsorted.length} remaining.</p>
        </div>

        {/* Unsorted items */}
        {!allSorted && (
          <div className="mb-10">
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-3">Unsorted</h3>
            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
              {unsorted.map(item => (
                <button
                  key={item.id}
                  onClick={() => setSelectedItem(item.id)}
                  className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm transition-all duration-200 active:scale-[0.97] ${
                    selectedItem === item.id
                      ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-md"
                      : "surface-raised border hover:shadow-sm"
                  }`}
                >
                  {item.text}
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Category selection for selected item */}
        {selectedItem && (
          <div className="surface-warm rounded-xl p-6 mb-10 animate-fade-up">
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-4">
              Where does <strong>"{items.find(i => i.id === selectedItem)?.text}"</strong> belong?
            </p>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
              {categories.map(cat => (
                <button
                  key={cat.key}
                  onClick={() => assignCategory(selectedItem, cat.key)}
                  className={`flex items-center gap-3 p-4 rounded-xl border-2 transition-all duration-200 hover:shadow-sm active:scale-[0.97] ${cat.color}`}
                >
                  <cat.icon className="h-5 w-5" />
                  <div className="text-left">
                    <p className="font-semibold text-sm">{cat.label}</p>
                    <p className="text-xs opacity-70">{cat.desc}</p>
                  </div>
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Matrix grid */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 mb-10">
          {categories.map(cat => {
            const catItems = items.filter(i => i.category === cat.key);
            return (
              <div key={cat.key} className={`rounded-xl border-2 p-5 ${cat.color}`}>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
                  <cat.icon className="h-4 w-4" />
                  <h3 className="font-display font-semibold text-sm">{cat.label}</h3>
                  <span className="text-xs opacity-60">({catItems.length})</span>
                </div>
                <div className="space-y-1.5">
                  {catItems.map(item => (
                    <p key={item.id} className="text-sm py-1">{item.text}</p>
                  ))}
                  {catItems.length === 0 && (
                    <p className="text-xs opacity-40 py-2">No items yet</p>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        <div className="flex justify-end">
          <Button variant="hero" size="lg" onClick={onContinue} disabled={!allSorted}>
            {allSorted ? "Set Weekly Outcomes" : `Sort ${unsorted.length} more items`}
            <ArrowRight className="ml-2 h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

        <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">
          <span className="font-display font-semibold text-foreground">WeeklyFlow</span> · Built for people who think too much and plan too little.
        </div>
      </footer>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: ./src/components/NavLink.tsx

import { NavLink as RouterNavLink, NavLinkProps } from "react-router-dom";
import { forwardRef } from "react";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

interface NavLinkCompatProps extends Omit<NavLinkProps, "className"> {
  className?: string;
  activeClassName?: string;
  pendingClassName?: string;
}

const NavLink = forwardRef<HTMLAnchorElement, NavLinkCompatProps>(
  ({ className, activeClassName, pendingClassName, to, ...props }, ref) => {
    return (
      <RouterNavLink
        ref={ref}
        to={to}
        className={({ isActive, isPending }) =>
          cn(className, isActive && activeClassName, isPending && pendingClassName)
        }
        {...props}
      />
    );
  },
);

NavLink.displayName = "NavLink";

export { NavLink };

import { useState } from "react";

import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Check, Lock, Loader2, X, Crown } from "lucide-react";
import { useState } from "react";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { PRO_FEATURES, FREE_FEATURES } from "@/lib/plans";

interface PaywallScreenProps {
  expired: boolean;
  daysLeft: number;
  onUpgrade: () => Promise<void>;
  onBack?: () => void;
}

export function PaywallScreen({ expired, daysLeft, onUpgrade, onBack }: PaywallScreenProps) {
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleUpgrade = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      await onUpgrade();
    } catch {
      toast.error("Failed to open checkout. Please try again.");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background flex items-center justify-center px-6 py-12">
      <div className="max-w-3xl w-full animate-fade-up">
        <div className="text-center mb-10">
          <div className="w-14 h-14 rounded-2xl bg-destructive/10 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-5">
            <Lock className="h-6 w-6 text-destructive" />
          </div>
          <h2 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-2">
            {expired ? "Your Free Trial Has Ended" : "Unlock the Full Experience"}
          </h2>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground max-w-md mx-auto">
            {expired
              ? "Your 7-day free trial has expired. Upgrade to Pro to keep your data and unlock all features."
              : `You have ${daysLeft} day${daysLeft !== 1 ? "s" : ""} left. See what you're missing with Pro.`}
          </p>
        </div>

        <div className="grid sm:grid-cols-2 gap-6 mb-8">
          {/* Free Plan */}
          <div className="surface-raised rounded-2xl p-6 border opacity-75">
            <p className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">Free Plan</p>
            <p className="font-display text-3xl font-bold mb-1">$0</p>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-6">Limited features for 7 days.</p>

            <ul className="space-y-3 mb-6">
              {FREE_FEATURES.map((f) => (
                <li key={f} className="flex items-start gap-2 text-sm">
                  <Check className="h-4 w-4 text-success mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
                  <span>{f}</span>
                </li>
              ))}
            </ul>

            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-medium uppercase tracking-wider mb-3">Not included</p>
            <ul className="space-y-2">
              {PRO_FEATURES.slice(0, 4).map((f) => (
                <li key={f} className="flex items-start gap-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                  <X className="h-4 w-4 text-destructive/60 mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
                  <span>{f}</span>
                </li>
              ))}
            </ul>
          </div>

          {/* Pro Plan */}
          <div className="surface-raised rounded-2xl p-6 border-2 border-primary relative">
            <div className="absolute -top-3 left-6 bg-primary text-primary-foreground text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1 rounded-full flex items-center gap-1">
              <Crown className="h-3 w-3" /> Pro
            </div>
            <p className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">Pro Plan</p>
            <div className="flex items-baseline gap-1 mb-1">
              <span className="font-display text-3xl font-bold">$5</span>
              <span className="text-muted-foreground text-sm">/month</span>
            </div>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-6">Everything. Unlimited. No restrictions.</p>

            <Button variant="hero" className="w-full mb-6" size="lg" onClick={handleUpgrade} disabled={loading}>
              {loading ? <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" /> : "Upgrade to Pro"}
            </Button>

            <ul className="space-y-3">
              {[...FREE_FEATURES, ...PRO_FEATURES].map((f) => (
                <li key={f} className="flex items-start gap-2 text-sm">
                  <Check className="h-4 w-4 text-success mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
                  <span>{f.replace("Up to 10 brain dump items per week", "Unlimited brain dump items")}</span>
                </li>
              ))}

        {onBack && (
          <Button variant="ghost" className="w-full" onClick={onBack}>
            Go Back

        )}

  );

FILE: ./src/components/WeeklyClose.tsx

import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Check, ArrowRight, ArrowLeft, BarChart3, Trophy, Target, Repeat } from "lucide-react";
import { BrainDumpItem, WeeklyEntry } from "@/lib/store";

interface WeeklyCloseProps {
  items: BrainDumpItem[];
  week: WeeklyEntry;
  onCarryForward: (itemIds: string[]) => void;
  onClose: (droppedIds: string[]) => void;
  onBack?: () => void;
}

export function WeeklyClose({ items, week, onCarryForward, onClose, onBack }: WeeklyCloseProps) {
  const weekItems = items.filter(i => i.weekId === week.weekId);
  const completed = weekItems.filter(i => i.status === 'done');
  const remaining = weekItems.filter(i => i.status === 'pending');
  const intentional = weekItems.filter(i => i.source === 'intentional');
  const reactive = weekItems.filter(i => i.source === 'reactive');
  const completionRate = weekItems.length > 0 ? Math.round((completed.length / weekItems.length) * 100) : 0;

  const handleClose = () => {
    onClose(remaining.map(i => i.id));
  };

  const handleCarry = () => {
    onCarryForward(remaining.map(i => i.id));
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background px-6 py-12">
      <div className="max-w-2xl mx-auto">
        <div className="text-center mb-10 animate-fade-up">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-3 mb-2">
            {onBack && (
              <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={onBack}>
                <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
              </Button>
            )}
            <h2 className="text-3xl font-bold">Saturday Close</h2>
          </div>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground">Your week in review.</p>
        </div>

        {/* Stats */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-10">
          {[
            { label: "Completed", value: completed.length, icon: Check, color: "text-success" },
            { label: "Remaining", value: remaining.length, icon: Target, color: "text-muted-foreground" },
            { label: "Intentional", value: intentional.length, icon: BarChart3, color: "text-primary" },
            { label: "Reactive", value: reactive.length, icon: Repeat, color: "text-warning" },
          ].map((stat, i) => (
            <div key={stat.label} className="surface-raised rounded-xl p-5 text-center animate-fade-up" style={{ animationDelay: `${i * 0.08}s` }}>
              <stat.icon className={`h-5 w-5 mx-auto mb-2 ${stat.color}`} />
              <p className="font-display text-2xl font-bold">{stat.value}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{stat.label}</p>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Completion rate */}
        <div className="surface-warm rounded-xl p-6 mb-8 text-center animate-fade-up stagger-3">
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-2">Completion Rate</p>
          <p className="font-display text-5xl font-bold text-primary mb-2">{completionRate}%</p>
          <div className="w-full h-2 bg-border rounded-full overflow-hidden">
            <div className="h-full bg-primary rounded-full transition-all duration-700" style={{ width: `${completionRate}%` }} />
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Wins */}
        {week.wins.length > 0 && (
          <div className="mb-8 animate-fade-up stagger-4">
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-3 flex items-center gap-2">
              <Trophy className="h-4 w-4 text-accent" /> Wins This Week
            </h3>
            <div className="space-y-2">
              {week.wins.map((w, i) => (
                <div key={i} className="surface-raised rounded-lg px-4 py-3 text-sm">{w}</div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Remaining items */}
        {remaining.length > 0 && (
          <div className="mb-10 animate-fade-up stagger-5">
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-3">Still Open</h3>
            <div className="space-y-2">
              {remaining.map(item => (
                <div key={item.id} className="surface-raised rounded-lg px-4 py-3 text-sm flex items-center justify-between">
                  <span>{item.text}</span>
                  <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{item.category}</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 justify-end">
          {remaining.length > 0 && (
            <Button variant="hero-outline" size="lg" onClick={handleCarry}>
              Carry to Next Week <ArrowRight className="ml-2 h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
          )}
          <Button variant="hero" size="lg" onClick={handleClose}>
            Close Week & Start Fresh <Check className="ml-2 h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: ./src/components/WeeklySetup.tsx

import { useState } from "react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { ArrowRight, ArrowLeft, Target, Pen } from "lucide-react";

interface WeeklySetupProps {
  onComplete: (outcomes: string[], intention: string) => void;
  previousIntention?: string;
  onBack?: () => void;
}

export function WeeklySetup({ onComplete, previousIntention, onBack }: WeeklySetupProps) {
  const [outcomes, setOutcomes] = useState<string[]>(["", "", ""]);
  const [intention, setIntention] = useState("");
  const [step, setStep] = useState(previousIntention ? 0 : 1);

  const updateOutcome = (i: number, val: string) => {
    const updated = [...outcomes];
    updated[i] = val;
    setOutcomes(updated);
  };

  const validOutcomes = outcomes.filter(o => o.trim()).length >= 1;

  if (step === 0 && previousIntention) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background flex items-center justify-center px-6 py-12">
        <div className="max-w-lg w-full text-center animate-fade-up">
          <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-6">Reflecting on Last Week</h1>
          <div className="surface-warm rounded-xl p-6 mb-8 text-left">
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-2">Last Sunday you intended to:</p>
            <p className="font-display text-lg font-semibold italic">"{previousIntention}"</p>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-4">How did that go? Take a moment to reflect before planning this week.</p>
          </div>
          <Button variant="hero" size="lg" onClick={() => setStep(1)}>
            Continue to This Week <ArrowRight className="ml-2 h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (step === 1) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background flex items-center justify-center px-6 py-12">
        <div className="max-w-lg w-full animate-fade-up">
          <div className="text-center mb-10">
            <div className="w-14 h-14 rounded-2xl bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-5">
              <Target className="h-6 w-6 text-primary" />
            </div>
            <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-2">Three Outcomes</h1>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground">What does a successful week look like?</p>
          </div>

          <div className="space-y-4 mb-10">
            {outcomes.map((o, i) => (
              <div key={i}>
                <label htmlFor={`outcome-${i}`} className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground mb-1.5 block">Outcome {i + 1}</label>
                <input
                  id={`outcome-${i}`}
                  type="text"
                  value={o}
                  onChange={e => updateOutcome(i, e.target.value)}
                  placeholder={
                    i === 0 ? "e.g. Finish the project proposal" :
                    i === 1 ? "e.g. Exercise three times" :
                    "e.g. Have a proper conversation with a friend"
                  }
                  className="w-full h-12 px-4 rounded-lg border bg-background text-foreground font-body placeholder:text-muted-foreground"
                />
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>

          <div className="flex justify-end">
            <Button variant="hero" size="lg" onClick={() => setStep(2)} disabled={!validOutcomes}>
              Set Intention <ArrowRight className="ml-2 h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background flex items-center justify-center px-6 py-12">
      <div className="max-w-lg w-full animate-fade-up">
        <div className="text-center mb-10">
          <div className="w-14 h-14 rounded-2xl bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-5">
            <Pen className="h-6 w-6 text-primary" />
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-2">Weekly Intention</h1>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground">One sentence — how do you want to show up this week?</p>
        </div>

        <label htmlFor="weekly-intention" className="sr-only">Weekly intention</label>
        <textarea
          id="weekly-intention"
          value={intention}
          onChange={e => setIntention(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="e.g. I want to stay calm under pressure and not rush through things"
          rows={3}
          className="w-full p-4 rounded-lg border bg-background text-foreground font-body placeholder:text-muted-foreground resize-none mb-10"
        />

        <div className="flex justify-end">
          <Button
            variant="hero"
            size="lg"
            onClick={() => onComplete(outcomes.filter(o => o.trim()), intention.trim())}
            disabled={!intention.trim()}
          >
            Start Your Week <ArrowRight className="ml-2 h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


========================================
FILE: ./src/contexts/AuthContext.tsx
========================================

import { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, useCallback, type ReactNode } from "react";
import { supabase } from "@/integrations/supabase/client";
import type { User, Session } from "@supabase/supabase-js";

interface AuthState {
  user: User | null;
  session: Session | null;
  loading: boolean;
  subscribed: boolean;
  subscriptionEnd: string | null;
  checkingSubscription: boolean;
}

interface AuthContextValue extends AuthState {
  signUp: (email: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
  signIn: (email: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
  signOut: () => Promise<void>;
  checkSubscription: () => Promise<void>;
  createCheckout: () => Promise<void>;
}

const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextValue | null>(null);

export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  const [state, setState] = useState<AuthState>({
    user: null,
    session: null,
    loading: true,
    subscribed: false,
    subscriptionEnd: null,
    checkingSubscription: false,
  });

  const checkSubscription = useCallback(async () => {
    setState(prev => ({ ...prev, checkingSubscription: true }));
    try {
      const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke("check-subscription");
      if (error) throw error;
      setState(prev => ({
        ...prev,
        subscribed: data?.subscribed ?? false,
        subscriptionEnd: data?.subscription_end ?? null,
        checkingSubscription: false,
      }));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Failed to check subscription:", err);
      setState(prev => ({ ...prev, checkingSubscription: false }));
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event, session) => {
      setState(prev => ({
        ...prev,
        session,
        user: session?.user ?? null,
        loading: false,
      }));
      if (session?.user) {
        setTimeout(() => checkSubscription(), 0);
      } else {
        setState(prev => ({ ...prev, subscribed: false, subscriptionEnd: null }));
      }
    });

    supabase.auth.getSession().then(({ data: { session } }) => {
      setState(prev => ({
        ...prev,
        session,
        user: session?.user ?? null,
        loading: false,
      }));
      if (session?.user) {
        checkSubscription();
      }
    }).catch(() => {
      setState(prev => ({ ...prev, loading: false }));
    });

    // Safety timeout: if auth never resolves, stop loading after 5s
    const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
      setState(prev => {
        if (prev.loading) return { ...prev, loading: false };
        return prev;
      });
    }, 5000);

    return () => {
      subscription.unsubscribe();
      clearTimeout(timeout);
    };
  }, [checkSubscription]);

  // Periodic subscription check every 60s
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!state.user) return;
    const interval = setInterval(checkSubscription, 60_000);
    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, [state.user, checkSubscription]);

  const signUp = async (email: string, password: string) => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({ email, password });
    return { error: error ? new Error(error.message) : null };
  };

  const signIn = async (email: string, password: string) => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
    return { error: error ? new Error(error.message) : null };
  };

  const signOut = async () => {
    await supabase.auth.signOut();
  };

  const createCheckout = async () => {
    try {
      console.log("[CHECKOUT] Invoking create-checkout...");
      const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke("create-checkout", {
        body: { return_url: window.location.origin },
      });
      console.log("[CHECKOUT] Response:", { data, error });
      if (error) throw error;
      if (data?.url) {
        window.open(data.url, "_blank");
      } else {
        throw new Error("No checkout URL returned");
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Failed to create checkout:", err);
      throw err;
    }
  };

  return (
    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ ...state, signUp, signIn, signOut, checkSubscription, createCheckout }}>
      {children}
    </AuthContext.Provider>
  );
}

export function useAuth() {
  const ctx = useContext(AuthContext);
  if (!ctx) throw new Error("useAuth must be used within AuthProvider");
  return ctx;
}


========================================
FILE: ./src/hooks/use-mobile.tsx
========================================

import * as React from "react";

const MOBILE_BREAKPOINT = 768;

export function useIsMobile() {
  const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = React.useState<boolean | undefined>(undefined);

  React.useEffect(() => {
    const mql = window.matchMedia(`(max-width: ${MOBILE_BREAKPOINT - 1}px)`);
    const onChange = () => {
      setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT);
    };
    mql.addEventListener("change", onChange);
    setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT);
    return () => mql.removeEventListener("change", onChange);
  }, []);

  return !!isMobile;
}


========================================
FILE: ./src/hooks/use-toast.ts
========================================

import * as React from "react";

import type { ToastActionElement, ToastProps } from "@/components/ui/toast";

const TOAST_LIMIT = 1;
const TOAST_REMOVE_DELAY = 1000000;

type ToasterToast = ToastProps & {
  id: string;
  title?: React.ReactNode;
  description?: React.ReactNode;
  action?: ToastActionElement;
};

const actionTypes = {
  ADD_TOAST: "ADD_TOAST",
  UPDATE_TOAST: "UPDATE_TOAST",
  DISMISS_TOAST: "DISMISS_TOAST",
  REMOVE_TOAST: "REMOVE_TOAST",
} as const;

let count = 0;

function genId() {
  count = (count + 1) % Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
  return count.toString();
}

type ActionType = typeof actionTypes;

type Action =
  | {
      type: ActionType["ADD_TOAST"];
      toast: ToasterToast;
    }
  | {
      type: ActionType["UPDATE_TOAST"];
      toast: Partial<ToasterToast>;
    }
  | {
      type: ActionType["DISMISS_TOAST"];
      toastId?: ToasterToast["id"];
    }
  | {
      type: ActionType["REMOVE_TOAST"];
      toastId?: ToasterToast["id"];
    };

interface State {
  toasts: ToasterToast[];
}

const toastTimeouts = new Map<string, ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>>();

const addToRemoveQueue = (toastId: string) => {
  if (toastTimeouts.has(toastId)) {
    return;
  }

  const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
    toastTimeouts.delete(toastId);
    dispatch({
      type: "REMOVE_TOAST",
      toastId: toastId,
    });
  }, TOAST_REMOVE_DELAY);

  toastTimeouts.set(toastId, timeout);
};

export const reducer = (state: State, action: Action): State => {
  switch (action.type) {
    case "ADD_TOAST":
      return {
        ...state,
        toasts: [action.toast, ...state.toasts].slice(0, TOAST_LIMIT),
      };

    case "UPDATE_TOAST":
      return {
        ...state,
        toasts: state.toasts.map((t) => (t.id === action.toast.id ? { ...t, ...action.toast } : t)),
      };

    case "DISMISS_TOAST": {
      const { toastId } = action;

      // ! Side effects ! - This could be extracted into a dismissToast() action,
      // but I'll keep it here for simplicity
      if (toastId) {
        addToRemoveQueue(toastId);
      } else {
        state.toasts.forEach((toast) => {
          addToRemoveQueue(toast.id);
        });
      }

      return {
        ...state,
        toasts: state.toasts.map((t) =>
          t.id === toastId || toastId === undefined
            ? {
                ...t,
                open: false,
              }
            : t,
        ),
      };
    }
    case "REMOVE_TOAST":
      if (action.toastId === undefined) {
        return {
          ...state,
          toasts: [],
        };
      }
      return {
        ...state,
        toasts: state.toasts.filter((t) => t.id !== action.toastId),
      };
  }
};

const listeners: Array<(state: State) => void> = [];

let memoryState: State = { toasts: [] };

function dispatch(action: Action) {
  memoryState = reducer(memoryState, action);
  listeners.forEach((listener) => {
    listener(memoryState);
  });
}

type Toast = Omit<ToasterToast, "id">;

function toast({ ...props }: Toast) {
  const id = genId();

  const update = (props: ToasterToast) =>
    dispatch({
      type: "UPDATE_TOAST",
      toast: { ...props, id },
    });
  const dismiss = () => dispatch({ type: "DISMISS_TOAST", toastId: id });

  dispatch({
    type: "ADD_TOAST",
    toast: {
      ...props,
      id,
      open: true,
      onOpenChange: (open) => {
        if (!open) dismiss();
      },
    },
  });

  return {
    id: id,
    dismiss,
    update,
  };
}

function useToast() {
  const [state, setState] = React.useState<State>(memoryState);

  React.useEffect(() => {
    listeners.push(setState);
    return () => {
      const index = listeners.indexOf(setState);
      if (index > -1) {
        listeners.splice(index, 1);
      }
    };
  }, [state]);

  return {
    ...state,
    toast,
    dismiss: (toastId?: string) => dispatch({ type: "DISMISS_TOAST", toastId }),
  };
}

export { useToast, toast };

// Feature gating for Free vs Pro plans

export const FREE_PLAN_LIMITS = {
  maxBrainDumpItems: 10,
  maxDaily3: 3,
  hasEisenhowerMatrix: false,
  hasEveningReflection: false,
  hasWeeklyClose: false,
  hasWeeklyStats: false,
  hasDimensionTracking: false,
  hasShareableSummary: false,
  hasPersonalisedInsights: false,
} as const;

export const PRO_FEATURES = [
  "Unlimited brain dump items",
  "Eisenhower matrix sorting",
  "Evening reflection & win logging",
  "Saturday weekly close with stats",
  "Week in Numbers dashboard",
  "Personalised weekly insights",
  "Dimension tracking (exhaustion, cynicism, self-doubt)",
  "Shareable weekly summary card",
] as const;

export const FREE_FEATURES = [
  "Up to 10 brain dump items per week",
  "Daily 3 + Commander's Intent",
  "Morning focus session",
  "Sunday weekly setup",
  "Basic weekly rhythm",
] as const;

export function isFeatureLocked(feature: keyof typeof FREE_PLAN_LIMITS, isPro: boolean): boolean {
  if (isPro) return false;
  const value = FREE_PLAN_LIMITS[feature];
  return typeof value === 'boolean' ? !value : false;
}

export function getBrainDumpLimit(isPro: boolean): number {
  return isPro ? Infinity : FREE_PLAN_LIMITS.maxBrainDumpItems;
}


========================================
FILE: ./src/lib/store.ts

// Local storage-based state management for the planning app

export type EisenhowerCategory = 'do' | 'schedule' | 'delegate' | 'drop';
export type TaskStatus = 'pending' | 'done' | 'partial' | 'not-done';
export type TaskSource = 'intentional' | 'reactive';

export interface BrainDumpItem {
  id: string;
  text: string;
  category?: EisenhowerCategory;
  layer?: 'work' | 'personal' | 'avoiding' | 'worry';
  source: TaskSource;
  status: TaskStatus;
  createdAt: string;
  weekId: string;
}

export interface DailyEntry {
  date: string;
  daily3: string[]; // ids of brain dump items
  commandersIntent: string;
  win: string;
  completed: boolean;
}

export interface WeeklyEntry {
  weekId: string;
  startDate: string;
  outcomes: string[];
  intention: string;
  dimensions?: {
    exhaustion: number;
    cynicism: number;
    selfDoubt: number;
  };
  wins: string[];
  dailyEntries: DailyEntry[];
}

export interface AppState {
  onboarded: boolean;
  trialStartDate: string | null;
  isPaid: boolean;
  morningReminder: string;
  eveningReminder: string;
  currentWeekId: string | null;
  brainDump: BrainDumpItem[];
  weeks: WeeklyEntry[];
  currentView: string;
}

const DEFAULT_STATE: AppState = {
  onboarded: false,
  trialStartDate: null,
  isPaid: false,
  morningReminder: '07:00',
  eveningReminder: '21:00',
  currentWeekId: null,
  brainDump: [],
  weeks: [],
  currentView: 'landing',
};

const STORAGE_KEY = 'weekly-planning-app';

export function loadState(): AppState {
  try {
    const raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
    if (raw) return { ...DEFAULT_STATE, ...JSON.parse(raw) };
  } catch {}
  return { ...DEFAULT_STATE };
}

export function saveState(state: AppState) {
  localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(state));
}

export function generateId(): string {
  return Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10);
}

export function getWeekId(date: Date = new Date()): string {
  const d = new Date(date);
  d.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  const day = d.getDay();
  const diff = d.getDate() - day;
  d.setDate(diff);
  return d.toISOString().split('T')[0];
}

export function getTrialDaysRemaining(trialStart: string | null): number {
  if (!trialStart) return 7;
  const start = new Date(trialStart);
  const now = new Date();
  const diff = Math.floor((now.getTime() - start.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
  return Math.max(0, 7 - diff);
}

import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge";

export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {

}

FILE: ./src/pages/Index.tsx

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback, lazy, Suspense } from "react";

import { LandingPage } from "@/components/LandingPage";
const OnboardingFlow = lazy(() => import("@/components/OnboardingFlow").then(m => ({ default: m.OnboardingFlow })));
const BrainDump = lazy(() => import("@/components/BrainDump").then(m => ({ default: m.BrainDump })));
const EisenhowerMatrix = lazy(() => import("@/components/EisenhowerMatrix").then(m => ({ default: m.EisenhowerMatrix })));
const WeeklySetup = lazy(() => import("@/components/WeeklySetup").then(m => ({ default: m.WeeklySetup })));
const DailyView = lazy(() => import("@/components/DailyView").then(m => ({ default: m.DailyView })));
const WeeklyClose = lazy(() => import("@/components/WeeklyClose").then(m => ({ default: m.WeeklyClose })));
const AppDashboard = lazy(() => import("@/components/AppDashboard").then(m => ({ default: m.AppDashboard })));
const PaywallScreen = lazy(() => import("@/components/PaywallScreen").then(m => ({ default: m.PaywallScreen })));
const AuthScreen = lazy(() => import("@/components/AuthScreen").then(m => ({ default: m.AuthScreen })));
import { useAuth } from "@/contexts/AuthContext";
import {
  AppState, loadState, saveState, getWeekId, generateId,
  BrainDumpItem, WeeklyEntry, DailyEntry, getTrialDaysRemaining,
} from "@/lib/store";
import { isFeatureLocked, getBrainDumpLimit } from "@/lib/plans";
import { toast } from "sonner";

const LoadingFallback = () => (
  <div className="min-h-screen bg-background flex items-center justify-center">
    <div className="animate-pulse text-muted-foreground">Loading...</div>
  </div>
);

const Index = () => {
  const { user, loading: authLoading, subscribed, createCheckout, checkSubscription, signOut } = useAuth();
  const [state, setState] = useState<AppState>(loadState);

  useEffect(() => {
    saveState(state);
  }, [state]);

  // Check subscription on checkout return
  useEffect(() => {
    const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    if (params.get("checkout") === "success") {
      checkSubscription();
      toast.success("Payment successful! You now have full access.");
      window.history.replaceState({}, "", "/");
    }
  }, [checkSubscription]);

  // Sync subscription status to local state
  useEffect(() => {
    if (subscribed && !state.isPaid) {
      setState(prev => ({ ...prev, isPaid: true }));
    }
  }, [subscribed, state.isPaid]);

  // Handle "Buy Now" → auth → checkout flow
  useEffect(() => {
    if (user && state.currentView === 'auth-checkout') {
      if (!state.onboarded) {
        setState(prev => ({ ...prev, onboarded: true, trialStartDate: new Date().toISOString(), currentView: 'dashboard' }));
      } else {
        setState(prev => ({ ...prev, currentView: 'dashboard' }));
      }
      setTimeout(() => createCheckout(), 500);
    }
  }, [user, state.currentView, state.onboarded, createCheckout]);

  // Auto-redirect after auth
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!authLoading && user && !state.onboarded && state.currentView !== 'auth-checkout' && state.currentView !== 'onboarding') {
      setState(prev => ({ ...prev, currentView: 'onboarding' }));
    } else if (!authLoading && user && state.onboarded && (state.currentView === 'landing' || state.currentView === 'auth')) {
      setState(prev => ({ ...prev, currentView: 'dashboard' }));
    }
  }, [user, authLoading, state.onboarded, state.currentView]);

  const update = useCallback((partial: Partial<AppState>) => {
    setState(prev => ({ ...prev, ...partial }));
  }, []);

  const weekId = getWeekId();
  const currentWeek = state.weeks.find(w => w.weekId === weekId);
  const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
  const dayOfWeek = new Date().getDay();
  const todayEntry = currentWeek?.dailyEntries.find(d => d.date === today) || null;
  const daysLeft = getTrialDaysRemaining(state.trialStartDate);
  const trialExpired = state.onboarded && !state.isPaid && !subscribed && daysLeft <= 0;
  const isPro = state.isPaid || subscribed;

  const handleUpgrade = async () => {
    await createCheckout();
  };

  const handleSignOut = async () => {
    await signOut();
    update({ currentView: 'landing' });
  };

  // Show loading while auth initializes
  if (authLoading) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background flex items-center justify-center">
        <div className="animate-pulse text-muted-foreground">Loading...</div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  // Landing — show if not logged in and not onboarded
  if (!user && (state.currentView === 'landing' || (!state.onboarded && state.currentView !== 'auth' && state.currentView !== 'auth-checkout'))) {
    return (
      <LandingPage
        onStart={() => update({ currentView: 'auth' })}
        onBuyNow={() => update({ currentView: 'auth-checkout' })}
      />
    );
  }

  // Auth screen (auth-checkout means: after auth, go straight to checkout)
  if ((state.currentView === 'auth' || state.currentView === 'auth-checkout' || (!user && state.onboarded)) && !user) {
    return <Suspense fallback={<LoadingFallback />}><AuthScreen onBack={() => update({ currentView: 'landing' })} /></Suspense>;
  }




  // Onboarding
  if (state.currentView === 'onboarding') {
    return (
      <Suspense fallback={<LoadingFallback />}>
        <OnboardingFlow
          onComplete={(morning, evening) => {
            update({
              onboarded: true,
              trialStartDate: new Date().toISOString(),
              morningReminder: morning,
              eveningReminder: evening,
              currentView: 'braindump',
              currentWeekId: weekId,
            });
          }}
        />
      </Suspense>
    );
  }

  // Paywall screen (explicit navigation or trial expired)
  if (state.currentView === 'paywall' || trialExpired) {
    return (
      <Suspense fallback={<LoadingFallback />}>
        <PaywallScreen
          expired={trialExpired}
          daysLeft={daysLeft}
          onUpgrade={handleUpgrade}
          onBack={!trialExpired ? () => update({ currentView: 'dashboard' }) : undefined}
        />
      </Suspense>
    );
  }

  // Brain Dump
  if (state.currentView === 'braindump') {
    return (
      <Suspense fallback={<LoadingFallback />}>
        <BrainDump
          items={state.brainDump}
          weekId={weekId}
          isPro={isPro}
          onUpdate={(items) => update({ brainDump: items })}
          onContinue={() => update({ currentView: 'matrix' })}
          onBack={() => update({ currentView: 'dashboard' })}
        />
      </Suspense>
    );
  }

  // Brain Dump (reactive)
  if (state.currentView === 'braindump-reactive') {
    return (
      <Suspense fallback={<LoadingFallback />}>
        <BrainDump
          items={state.brainDump}
          weekId={weekId}
          isPro={isPro}
          onUpdate={(items) => update({ brainDump: items })}
          onContinue={() => update({ currentView: 'daily' })}
          onBack={() => update({ currentView: 'daily' })}
          isReactive
        />
      </Suspense>
    );
  }

  // Eisenhower Matrix (Pro only — free users skip to weekly setup)
  if (state.currentView === 'matrix') {
    if (!isPro) {
      // Redirect free users to weekly setup, skipping matrix
      update({ currentView: 'weekly-setup' });
      return <LoadingFallback />;
    }
    return (
      <Suspense fallback={<LoadingFallback />}>
        <EisenhowerMatrix
          items={state.brainDump.filter(i => i.weekId === weekId)}
          onUpdate={(updated) => {
            const otherItems = state.brainDump.filter(i => i.weekId !== weekId);
            update({ brainDump: [...otherItems, ...updated] });
          }}
          onContinue={() => update({ currentView: 'weekly-setup' })}
          onBack={() => update({ currentView: 'braindump' })}
        />
      </Suspense>
    );
  }

  // Weekly Setup
  if (state.currentView === 'weekly-setup' || state.currentView === 'sunday') {
    const prevWeek = state.weeks[state.weeks.length - 1];
    return (
      <Suspense fallback={<LoadingFallback />}>
        <WeeklySetup
          previousIntention={prevWeek?.intention}
          onComplete={(outcomes, intention) => {
            const newWeek: WeeklyEntry = {
              weekId,
              startDate: new Date().toISOString(),
              outcomes,
              intention,
              wins: [],
              dailyEntries: [],
            };
            const existingIdx = state.weeks.findIndex(w => w.weekId === weekId);
            const weeks = [...state.weeks];
            if (existingIdx >= 0) {
              weeks[existingIdx] = { ...weeks[existingIdx], outcomes, intention };
            } else {
              weeks.push(newWeek);
            }
            update({ weeks, currentView: 'dashboard', currentWeekId: weekId });
          }}
          onBack={() => update({ currentView: 'dashboard' })}
        />
      </Suspense>
    );
  }

  // Daily View
  if (state.currentView === 'daily') {
    return (
      <Suspense fallback={<LoadingFallback />}>
        <DailyView
          items={state.brainDump.filter(i => i.weekId === weekId && i.status === 'pending')}
          dailyEntry={todayEntry}
          onSaveEntry={(entry) => {
            const weeks = state.weeks.map(w => {
              if (w.weekId !== weekId) return w;
              const entries = w.dailyEntries.filter(d => d.date !== entry.date);
              entries.push(entry);
              const wins = entry.win ? [...w.wins, entry.win] : w.wins;
              return { ...w, dailyEntries: entries, wins };
            });
            update({ weeks });
          }}
          onUpdateItems={(items) => {
            const otherItems = state.brainDump.filter(i => i.weekId !== weekId);
            update({ brainDump: [...otherItems, ...items] });
          }}
          onAddReactive={() => update({ currentView: 'braindump-reactive' })}
          onBack={() => update({ currentView: 'dashboard' })}
        />
      </Suspense>
    );
  }

  // Saturday Close (Pro only)
  if (state.currentView === 'saturday') {
    if (!isPro) {
      update({ currentView: 'paywall' });
      return <LoadingFallback />;
    }
    if (!currentWeek) {
      return <LoadingFallback />;
    }
    return (
      <Suspense fallback={<LoadingFallback />}>
        <WeeklyClose
          items={state.brainDump}
          week={currentWeek}
          onCarryForward={(ids) => {
            const nextWeekId = getWeekId(new Date(Date.now() + 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
            const updated = state.brainDump.map(i =>
              ids.includes(i.id) ? { ...i, weekId: nextWeekId } : i
            );
            update({ brainDump: updated, currentView: 'dashboard' });
          }}
          onClose={() => {
            update({ currentView: 'dashboard' });
          }}
          onBack={() => update({ currentView: 'dashboard' })}
        />
      </Suspense>
    );
  }

  // Dashboard
  return (
    <Suspense fallback={<LoadingFallback />}>
      <AppDashboard
        trialStart={state.trialStartDate}
        dayOfWeek={dayOfWeek}
        isPaid={state.isPaid || subscribed}
        onNavigate={(view) => update({ currentView: view })}
        onSignOut={handleSignOut}
      />
    </Suspense>
  );
};

export default Index;

import { useLocation } from "react-router-dom";
import { useEffect } from "react";

const NotFound = () => {
  const location = useLocation();

  useEffect(() => {
    document.title = "Page Not Found | WeeklyFlow";
    console.error("404 Error: User attempted to access non-existent route:", location.pathname);
  }, [location.pathname]);

  return (
    <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-muted">
      <div className="text-center">
        <h1 className="mb-4 text-4xl font-bold">404</h1>
        <p className="mb-4 text-xl text-muted-foreground">Oops! Page not found</p>
        <a href="/" className="text-primary underline hover:text-primary/90">
          Return to Home
        </a>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default NotFound;

========================================
FILE: ./supabase/functions/check-subscription/index.ts
========================================

import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std@0.190.0/http/server.ts";
import Stripe from "https://esm.sh/stripe@18.5.0";
import { createClient } from "npm:@supabase/supabase-js@2.57.2";

const corsHeaders = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type, x-supabase-client-platform, x-supabase-client-platform-version, x-supabase-client-runtime, x-supabase-client-runtime-version",
};

const logStep = (step: string, details?: any) => {
  const detailsStr = details ? ` - ${JSON.stringify(details)}` : '';
  console.log(`[CHECK-SUBSCRIPTION] ${step}${detailsStr}`);
};

serve(async (req) => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
    return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
  }

  const supabaseClient = createClient(
    Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_URL") ?? "",
    Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY") ?? "",
    { auth: { persistSession: false } }
  );

  try {
    logStep("Function started");

    const stripeKey = Deno.env.get("STRIPE_SECRET_KEY");
    if (!stripeKey) throw new Error("STRIPE_SECRET_KEY is not set");

    const authHeader = req.headers.get("Authorization");
    if (!authHeader) throw new Error("No authorization header provided");

    const token = authHeader.replace("Bearer ", "");
    const { data: userData, error: userError } = await supabaseClient.auth.getUser(token);
    if (userError) throw new Error(`Authentication error: ${userError.message}`);
    const user = userData.user;
    if (!user?.email) throw new Error("User not authenticated or email not available");
    logStep("User authenticated", { userId: user.id, email: user.email });

    const stripe = new Stripe(stripeKey, { apiVersion: "2025-08-27.basil" });
    const customers = await stripe.customers.list({ email: user.email, limit: 1 });

    if (customers.data.length === 0) {
      logStep("No customer found");
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ subscribed: false }), {
        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        status: 200,
      });
    }

    const customerId = customers.data[0].id;
    logStep("Found Stripe customer", { customerId });

    const subscriptions = await stripe.subscriptions.list({
      customer: customerId,
      status: "active",
      limit: 1,
    });

    const hasActiveSub = subscriptions.data.length > 0;
    let subscriptionEnd = null;

    if (hasActiveSub) {
      const subscription = subscriptions.data[0];
      subscriptionEnd = new Date(subscription.current_period_end * 1000).toISOString();
      logStep("Active subscription found", { subscriptionId: subscription.id });
    } else {
      logStep("No active subscription found");
    }

    return new Response(JSON.stringify({
      subscribed: hasActiveSub,
      subscription_end: subscriptionEnd,
    }), {
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      status: 200,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error);
    logStep("ERROR", { message: errorMessage });
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "An internal error occurred. Please try again." }), {
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      status: 500,
    });
  }
});


========================================
FILE: ./supabase/functions/create-checkout/index.ts
========================================

import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std@0.190.0/http/server.ts";
import Stripe from "https://esm.sh/stripe@18.5.0";
import { createClient } from "npm:@supabase/supabase-js@2.57.2";

const corsHeaders = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type, x-supabase-client-platform, x-supabase-client-platform-version, x-supabase-client-runtime, x-supabase-client-runtime-version",
};

serve(async (req) => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
    return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
  }

  const supabaseClient = createClient(
    Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_URL") ?? "",
    Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY") ?? "",
    { auth: { persistSession: false } }
  );

  try {
    const authHeader = req.headers.get("Authorization")!;
    const token = authHeader.replace("Bearer ", "");
    const { data } = await supabaseClient.auth.getUser(token);
    const user = data.user;
    if (!user?.email) throw new Error("User not authenticated or email not available");

    let returnUrl = req.headers.get("origin") || "https://weekly-wins-system.lovable.app";
    try {
      const body = await req.json();
      if (body?.return_url) returnUrl = body.return_url;
    } catch { /* no body */ }

    const stripe = new Stripe(Deno.env.get("STRIPE_SECRET_KEY") || "", {
      apiVersion: "2025-08-27.basil",
    });

    const customers = await stripe.customers.list({ email: user.email, limit: 1 });
    let customerId;
    if (customers.data.length > 0) {
      customerId = customers.data[0].id;
    }

    const session = await stripe.checkout.sessions.create({
      customer: customerId,
      customer_email: customerId ? undefined : user.email,
      payment_method_types: ['card'],
      line_items: [
        {
          price: "price_1TE2Td7ebJCGijgNz8RIlcrA",
          quantity: 1,
        },
      ],
      mode: "subscription",
      success_url: `${returnUrl}/?checkout=success`,
      cancel_url: `${returnUrl}/?checkout=canceled`,
    });

    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ url: session.url }), {
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      status: 200,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[CREATE-CHECKOUT] Error:", error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error));
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "An internal error occurred. Please try again." }), {
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      status: 500,
    });
  }
});
